# 不走 GitHub / 不用上传：复制本文件全部内容到宝塔终端执行
set -e
SERVICE="toolbox-admin"
APP="$(systemctl show "$SERVICE" -p WorkingDirectory --value 2>/dev/null || true)"
[ -n "$APP" ] && [ "$APP" != "/" ] || APP="/www/wwwroot/gjx.vst76.cn"
TS="$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)"
PKG="/tmp/toolbox-multithread-download-20260623-$TS.tar.gz"
B64="$PKG.b64"
TMP="/tmp/toolbox-multithread-download-20260623-$TS"
BACKUP="/www/backup/toolbox-multithread-download-20260623-$TS"
SHA="9a202021a56132cba869f9a921ce8cfc4b849b9802eac0458d440dcfe3785cbd"

mkdir -p "$TMP" "$BACKUP"
[ -d "$APP" ] || { echo "APP dir not found: $APP"; exit 1; }

cat > "$B64" <<'TOOLBOX_MULTITHREAD_DOWNLOAD_20260623_B64'

TOOLBOX_MULTITHREAD_DOWNLOAD_20260623_B64

if command -v base64 >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  base64 -d "$B64" > "$PKG"
else
  python3 -c 'import base64,pathlib,sys; pathlib.Path(sys.argv[2]).write_bytes(base64.b64decode(pathlib.Path(sys.argv[1]).read_text()))' "$B64" "$PKG"
fi

echo "$SHA  $PKG" | sha256sum -c -
tar -xzf "$PKG" -C "$TMP"
python3 -m py_compile "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/app.py"

cd "$APP"
cp -a app.py wwwroot client-template assets deploy admin-desktop-template "$BACKUP/" 2>/dev/null || true
rm -rf app.py wwwroot client-template assets deploy admin-desktop-template __pycache__ data/client-cache data/client-jobs
\cp -a "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/app.py" "$APP/app.py"
\cp -a "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/wwwroot" "$APP/wwwroot"
\cp -a "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/client-template" "$APP/client-template"
\cp -a "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/assets" "$APP/assets"
\cp -a "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/deploy" "$APP/deploy"
\cp -a "$TMP/ToolboxAdminApi-oneclick/admin-desktop-template" "$APP/admin-desktop-template"
if [ -d "$BACKUP/wwwroot/uploads" ]; then
  mkdir -p "$APP/wwwroot"
  rm -rf "$APP/wwwroot/uploads"
  \cp -a "$BACKUP/wwwroot/uploads" "$APP/wwwroot/uploads"
fi

systemctl restart "$SERVICE"
sleep 2
systemctl is-active --quiet "$SERVICE"
curl -fsS "http://127.0.0.1:5088/api/public/brand" >/dev/null
grep -q "MaxSegmentedDownloadConnections = 16" client-template/ToolboxClient.cs
grep -q "OpenProbeDownloadResponse" client-template/ToolboxClient.cs
grep -q "DefaultConnectionLimit = 96" client-template/ToolboxClient.cs
test ! -d data/client-cache || [ -z "$(ls -A data/client-cache 2>/dev/null)" ]
echo "OK: multi-thread segmented downloader updated. Re-download all three client EXEs in the admin backend. Backup: $BACKUP"
